<li><b>X. Shen</b>, Z. Gajic and J. A. Momoh, "The Recursive Reduced-Order Open-Loop Optimal Control of Discrete Weakly Coupled Linear Systems'', Proc. IEEE CECC '91, pp.75-78, Calgary, Alberta, April 8-10, 1991.</li>
